SQL Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) types\n\nmod data_type;\nmod ddl;\nmod operator;\nmod query;\nmod value;\nmod statement;\n#[cfg(not(feature = \"std\"))]\nuse alloc::{\n    boxed::Box,\n    string::{String, ToString},\n    vec::Vec,\n};\nuse core::fmt;\n\n#[cfg(feature = \"serde\")]\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n\npub use self::data_type::DataType;\npub use self::ddl::{\n    AlterTableOperation, ColumnDef, ColumnOption, ColumnOptionDef, ReferentialAction,\n    TableConstraint,\n};\npub use self::operator::{BinaryOperator, UnaryOperator};\npub use self::query::{\n    Cte, Fetch, Join, JoinConstraint, JoinOperator, LateralView, Offset, OffsetRows, OrderByExpr,\n    Query, Select, SelectItem, SetExpr, SetOperator, TableAlias, TableFactor, TableWithJoins, Top,\n    Values, With,\n};\npub use self::value::{DateTimeField, TrimWhereField, Value};\n\nstruct DisplaySeparated<'a, T>\nwhere\n    T: fmt::Display,\n{\n    slice: &'a [T],\n    sep: &'static str,\n}\n\nimpl<'a, T> fmt::Display for DisplaySeparated<'a, T>\nwhere\n    T: fmt::Display,\n{\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        let mut delim = \"\";\n        for t in self.slice {\n            write!(f, \"{}\", delim)?;\n            delim = self.sep;\n            write!(f, \"{}\", t)?;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\nfn display_separated<'a, T>(slice: &'a [T], sep: &'static str) -> DisplaySeparated<'a, T>\nwhere\n    T: fmt::Display,\n{\n    DisplaySeparated { slice, sep }\n}\n\nfn display_comma_separated<T>(slice: &[T]) -> DisplaySeparated<'_, T>\nwhere\n    T: fmt::Display,\n{\n    DisplaySeparated { slice, sep: \", \" }\n}\n\n/// An identifier, decomposed into its value or character data and the quote style.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct Ident {\n    /// The value of the identifier without quotes.\n    pub value: String,\n    /// The starting quote if any. Valid quote characters are the single quote,\n    /// double quote, backtick, and opening square bracket.\n    pub quote_style: Option<char>,\n}\n\nimpl Ident {\n    /// Create a new identifier with the given value and no quotes.\n    pub fn new<S>(value: S) -> Self\n    where\n        S: Into<String>,\n    {\n        Ident {\n            value: value.into(),\n            quote_style: None,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Create a new quoted identifier with the given quote and value. This function\n    /// panics if the given quote is not a valid quote character.\n    pub fn with_quote<S>(quote: char, value: S) -> Self\n    where\n        S: Into<String>,\n    {\n        assert!(quote == '\\'' || quote == '\"' || quote == '`' || quote == '[');\n        Ident {\n            value: value.into(),\n            quote_style: Some(quote),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl From<&str> for Ident {\n    fn from(value: &str) -> Self {\n        Ident {\n            value: value.to_string(),\n            quote_style: None,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for Ident {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        match self.quote_style {\n            Some(q) if q == '\"' || q == '\\'' || q == '`' => write!(f, \"{}{}{}\", q, self.value, q),\n            Some(q) if q == '[' => write!(f, \"[{}]\", self.value),\n            None => f.write_str(&self.value),\n            _ => panic!(\"unexpected quote style\"),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// A name of a table, view, custom type, etc., possibly multi-part, i.e. db.schema.obj\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct ObjectName(pub Vec<Ident>);\n\nimpl fmt::Display for ObjectName {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        write!(f, \"{}\", display_separated(&self.0, \".\"))\n    }\n}\n\n/// An SQL expression of any type.\n///\n/// The parser does not distinguish between expressions of different types\n/// (e.g. boolean vs string), so the caller must handle expressions of\n/// inappropriate type, like `WHERE 1` or `SELECT 1=1`, as necessary.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum Expr {\n    /// Identifier e.g. table name or column name\n    Identifier(Ident),\n    /// Unqualified wildcard (`*`). SQL allows this in limited contexts, such as:\n    /// - right after `SELECT` (which is represented as a [SelectItem::Wildcard] instead)\n    /// - or as part of an aggregate function, e.g. `COUNT(*)`,\n    ///\n    /// ...but we currently also accept it in contexts where it doesn't make\n    /// sense, such as `* + *`\n    Wildcard,\n    /// Qualified wildcard, e.g. `alias.*` or `schema.table.*`.\n    /// (Same caveats apply to `QualifiedWildcard` as to `Wildcard`.)\n    QualifiedWildcard(Vec<Ident>),\n    /// Multi-part identifier, e.g. `table_alias.column` or `schema.table.col`\n    CompoundIdentifier(Vec<Ident>),\n    /// `IS NULL` expression\n    IsNull(Box<Expr>),\n    /// `IS NOT NULL` expression\n    IsNotNull(Box<Expr>),\n    /// `[ NOT ] IN (val1, val2, ...)`\n    InList {\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n        list: Vec<Expr>,\n        negated: bool,\n    },\n    /// `[ NOT ] IN (SELECT ...)`\n    InSubquery {\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n        subquery: Box<Query>,\n        negated: bool,\n    },\n    /// `<expr> [ NOT ] BETWEEN <low> AND <high>`\n    Between {\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n        negated: bool,\n        low: Box<Expr>,\n        high: Box<Expr>,\n    },\n    /// Binary operation e.g. `1 + 1` or `foo > bar`\n    BinaryOp {\n        left: Box<Expr>,\n        op: BinaryOperator,\n        right: Box<Expr>,\n    },\n    /// Unary operation e.g. `NOT foo`\n    UnaryOp {\n        op: UnaryOperator,\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n    },\n    /// CAST an expression to a different data type e.g. `CAST(foo AS VARCHAR(123))`\n    Cast {\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n        data_type: DataType,\n    },\n    /// TRY_CAST an expression to a different data type e.g. `TRY_CAST(foo AS VARCHAR(123))`\n    //  this differs from CAST in the choice of how to implement invalid conversions\n    TryCast {\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n        data_type: DataType,\n    },\n    /// EXTRACT(DateTimeField FROM <expr>)\n    Extract {\n        field: DateTimeField,\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n    },\n    /// SUBSTRING(<expr> [FROM <expr>] [FOR <expr>])\n    Substring {\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n        substring_from: Option<Box<Expr>>,\n        substring_for: Option<Box<Expr>>,\n    },\n    /// TRIM([BOTH | LEADING | TRAILING] <expr> [FROM <expr>])\\\n    /// Or\\\n    /// TRIM(<expr>)\n    Trim {\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n        // ([BOTH | LEADING | TRAILING], <expr>)\n        trim_where: Option<(TrimWhereField, Box<Expr>)>,\n    },\n    /// `expr COLLATE collation`\n    Collate {\n        expr: Box<Expr>,\n        collation: ObjectName,\n    },\n    /// Nested expression e.g. `(foo > bar)` or `(1)`\n    Nested(Box<Expr>),\n    /// A literal value, such as string, number, date or NULL\n    Value(Value),\n    /// A constant of form `<data_type> 'value'`.\n    /// This can represent ANSI SQL `DATE`, `TIME`, and `TIMESTAMP` literals (such as `DATE '2020-01-01'`),\n    /// as well as constants of other types (a non-standard PostgreSQL extension).\n    TypedString {\n        data_type: DataType,\n        value: String,\n    },\n    MapAccess {\n        column: Box<Expr>,\n        key: String,\n    },\n    /// Scalar function call e.g. `LEFT(foo, 5)`\n    Function(Function),\n    /// `CASE [<operand>] WHEN <condition> THEN <result> ... [ELSE <result>] END`\n    ///\n    /// Note we only recognize a complete single expression as `<condition>`,\n    /// not `< 0` nor `1, 2, 3` as allowed in a `<simple when clause>` per\n    /// <https://jakewheat.github.io/sql-overview/sql-2011-foundation-grammar.html#simple-when-clause>\n    Case {\n        operand: Option<Box<Expr>>,\n        conditions: Vec<Expr>,\n        results: Vec<Expr>,\n        else_result: Option<Box<Expr>>,\n    },\n    /// An exists expression `EXISTS(SELECT ...)`, used in expressions like\n    /// `WHERE EXISTS (SELECT ...)`.\n    Exists(Box<Query>),\n    /// A parenthesized subquery `(SELECT ...)`, used in expression like\n    /// `SELECT (subquery) AS x` or `WHERE (subquery) = x`\n    Subquery(Box<Query>),\n    /// The `LISTAGG` function `SELECT LISTAGG(...) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY ...)`\n    ListAgg(ListAgg),\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for Expr {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            Expr::Identifier(s) => write!(f, \"{}\", s),\n            Expr::MapAccess { column, key } => write!(f, \"{}[\\\"{}\\\"]\", column, key),\n            Expr::Wildcard => f.write_str(\"*\"),\n            Expr::QualifiedWildcard(q) => write!(f, \"{}.*\", display_separated(q, \".\")),\n            Expr::CompoundIdentifier(s) => write!(f, \"{}\", display_separated(s, \".\")),\n            Expr::IsNull(ast) => write!(f, \"{} IS NULL\", ast),\n            Expr::IsNotNull(ast) => write!(f, \"{} IS NOT NULL\", ast),\n            Expr::InList {\n                expr,\n                list,\n                negated,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"{} {}IN ({})\",\n                expr,\n                if *negated { \"NOT \" } else { \"\" },\n                display_comma_separated(list)\n            ),\n            Expr::InSubquery {\n                expr,\n                subquery,\n                negated,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"{} {}IN ({})\",\n                expr,\n                if *negated { \"NOT \" } else { \"\" },\n                subquery\n            ),\n            Expr::Between {\n                expr,\n                negated,\n                low,\n                high,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"{} {}BETWEEN {} AND {}\",\n                expr,\n                if *negated { \"NOT \" } else { \"\" },\n                low,\n                high\n            ),\n            Expr::BinaryOp { left, op, right } => write!(f, \"{} {} {}\", left, op, right),\n            Expr::UnaryOp { op, expr } => {\n                if op == &UnaryOperator::PGPostfixFactorial {\n                    write!(f, \"{}{}\", expr, op)\n                } else {\n                    write!(f, \"{} {}\", op, expr)\n                }\n            }\n            Expr::Cast { expr, data_type } => write!(f, \"CAST({} AS {})\", expr, data_type),\n            Expr::TryCast { expr, data_type } => write!(f, \"TRY_CAST({} AS {})\", expr, data_type),\n            Expr::Extract { field, expr } => write!(f, \"EXTRACT({} FROM {})\", field, expr),\n            Expr::Collate { expr, collation } => write!(f, \"{} COLLATE {}\", expr, collation),\n            Expr::Nested(ast) => write!(f, \"({})\", ast),\n            Expr::Value(v) => write!(f, \"{}\", v),\n            Expr::TypedString { data_type, value } => {\n                write!(f, \"{}\", data_type)?;\n                write!(f, \" '{}'\", &value::escape_single_quote_string(value))\n            }\n            Expr::Function(fun) => write!(f, \"{}\", fun),\n            Expr::Case {\n                operand,\n                conditions,\n                results,\n                else_result,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"CASE\")?;\n                if let Some(operand) = operand {\n                    write!(f, \" {}\", operand)?;\n                }\n                for (c, r) in conditions.iter().zip(results) {\n                    write!(f, \" WHEN {} THEN {}\", c, r)?;\n                }\n\n                if let Some(else_result) = else_result {\n                    write!(f, \" ELSE {}\", else_result)?;\n                }\n                write!(f, \" END\")\n            }\n            Expr::Exists(s) => write!(f, \"EXISTS ({})\", s),\n            Expr::Subquery(s) => write!(f, \"({})\", s),\n            Expr::ListAgg(listagg) => write!(f, \"{}\", listagg),\n            Expr::Substring {\n                expr,\n                substring_from,\n                substring_for,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"SUBSTRING({}\", expr)?;\n                if let Some(from_part) = substring_from {\n                    write!(f, \" FROM {}\", from_part)?;\n                }\n                if let Some(from_part) = substring_for {\n                    write!(f, \" FOR {}\", from_part)?;\n                }\n\n                write!(f, \")\")\n            }\n            Expr::Trim { expr, trim_where } => {\n                write!(f, \"TRIM(\")?;\n                if let Some((ident, trim_char)) = trim_where {\n                    write!(f, \"{} {} FROM {}\", ident, trim_char, expr)?;\n                } else {\n                    write!(f, \"{}\", expr)?;\n                }\n\n                write!(f, \")\")\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// A window specification (i.e. `OVER (PARTITION BY .. ORDER BY .. etc.)`)\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct WindowSpec {\n    pub partition_by: Vec<Expr>,\n    pub order_by: Vec<OrderByExpr>,\n    pub window_frame: Option<WindowFrame>,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for WindowSpec {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        let mut delim = \"\";\n        if !self.partition_by.is_empty() {\n            delim = \" \";\n            write!(\n                f,\n                \"PARTITION BY {}\",\n                display_comma_separated(&self.partition_by)\n            )?;\n        }\n        if !self.order_by.is_empty() {\n            f.write_str(delim)?;\n            delim = \" \";\n            write!(f, \"ORDER BY {}\", display_comma_separated(&self.order_by))?;\n        }\n        if let Some(window_frame) = &self.window_frame {\n            if let Some(end_bound) = &window_frame.end_bound {\n                f.write_str(delim)?;\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"{} BETWEEN {} AND {}\",\n                    window_frame.units, window_frame.start_bound, end_bound\n                )?;\n            } else {\n                f.write_str(delim)?;\n                write!(f, \"{} {}\", window_frame.units, window_frame.start_bound)?;\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// Specifies the data processed by a window function, e.g.\n/// `RANGE UNBOUNDED PRECEDING` or `ROWS BETWEEN 5 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW`.\n///\n/// Note: The parser does not validate the specified bounds; the caller should\n/// reject invalid bounds like `ROWS UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING` before execution.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct WindowFrame {\n    pub units: WindowFrameUnits,\n    pub start_bound: WindowFrameBound,\n    /// The right bound of the `BETWEEN .. AND` clause. The end bound of `None`\n    /// indicates the shorthand form (e.g. `ROWS 1 PRECEDING`), which must\n    /// behave the same as `end_bound = WindowFrameBound::CurrentRow`.\n    pub end_bound: Option<WindowFrameBound>,\n    // TBD: EXCLUDE\n}\n\nimpl Default for WindowFrame {\n    /// returns default value for window frame\n    ///\n    /// see https://www.sqlite.org/windowfunctions.html#frame_specifications\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            units: WindowFrameUnits::Range,\n            start_bound: WindowFrameBound::Preceding(None),\n            end_bound: None,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum WindowFrameUnits {\n    Rows,\n    Range,\n    Groups,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for WindowFrameUnits {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        f.write_str(match self {\n            WindowFrameUnits::Rows => \"ROWS\",\n            WindowFrameUnits::Range => \"RANGE\",\n            WindowFrameUnits::Groups => \"GROUPS\",\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Specifies [WindowFrame]'s `start_bound` and `end_bound`\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum WindowFrameBound {\n    /// `CURRENT ROW`\n    CurrentRow,\n    /// `<N> PRECEDING` or `UNBOUNDED PRECEDING`\n    Preceding(Option<u64>),\n    /// `<N> FOLLOWING` or `UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING`.\n    Following(Option<u64>),\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for WindowFrameBound {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            WindowFrameBound::CurrentRow => f.write_str(\"CURRENT ROW\"),\n            WindowFrameBound::Preceding(None) => f.write_str(\"UNBOUNDED PRECEDING\"),\n            WindowFrameBound::Following(None) => f.write_str(\"UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING\"),\n            WindowFrameBound::Preceding(Some(n)) => write!(f, \"{} PRECEDING\", n),\n            WindowFrameBound::Following(Some(n)) => write!(f, \"{} FOLLOWING\", n),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum AddDropSync {\n    ADD,\n    DROP,\n    SYNC,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for AddDropSync {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            AddDropSync::SYNC => f.write_str(\"SYNC PARTITIONS\"),\n            AddDropSync::DROP => f.write_str(\"DROP PARTITIONS\"),\n            AddDropSync::ADD => f.write_str(\"ADD PARTITIONS\"),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum ShowCreateObject {\n    Event,\n    Function,\n    Procedure,\n    Table,\n    Trigger,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for ShowCreateObject {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            ShowCreateObject::Event => f.write_str(\"EVENT\"),\n            ShowCreateObject::Function => f.write_str(\"FUNCTION\"),\n            ShowCreateObject::Procedure => f.write_str(\"PROCEDURE\"),\n            ShowCreateObject::Table => f.write_str(\"TABLE\"),\n            ShowCreateObject::Trigger => f.write_str(\"TRIGGER\"),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// A top-level statement (SELECT, INSERT, CREATE, etc.)\n#[allow(clippy::large_enum_variant)]\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum Statement {\n    /// Analyze (Hive)\n    Analyze {\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        partitions: Option<Vec<Expr>>,\n        for_columns: bool,\n        columns: Vec<Ident>,\n        cache_metadata: bool,\n        noscan: bool,\n        compute_statistics: bool,\n    },\n    /// Truncate (Hive)\n    Truncate {\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        partitions: Option<Vec<Expr>>,\n    },\n    /// Msck (Hive)\n    Msck {\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        repair: bool,\n        partition_action: Option<AddDropSync>,\n    },\n    /// SELECT\n    Query(Box<Query>),\n    /// INSERT\n    Insert {\n        /// Only for Sqlite\n        or: Option<SqliteOnConflict>,\n        /// TABLE\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        /// COLUMNS\n        columns: Vec<Ident>,\n        /// Overwrite (Hive)\n        overwrite: bool,\n        /// A SQL query that specifies what to insert\n        source: Box<Query>,\n        /// partitioned insert (Hive)\n        partitioned: Option<Vec<Expr>>,\n        /// Columns defined after PARTITION\n        after_columns: Vec<Ident>,\n        /// whether the insert has the table keyword (Hive)\n        table: bool,\n    },\n    // TODO: Support ROW FORMAT\n    Directory {\n        overwrite: bool,\n        local: bool,\n        path: String,\n        file_format: Option<FileFormat>,\n        source: Box<Query>,\n    },\n    Copy {\n        /// TABLE\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        /// COLUMNS\n        columns: Vec<Ident>,\n        /// VALUES a vector of values to be copied\n        values: Vec<Option<String>>,\n    },\n    /// UPDATE\n    Update {\n        /// TABLE\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        /// Column assignments\n        assignments: Vec<Assignment>,\n        /// WHERE\n        selection: Option<Expr>,\n    },\n    /// DELETE\n    Delete {\n        /// FROM\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        /// WHERE\n        selection: Option<Expr>,\n    },\n    /// CREATE VIEW\n    CreateView {\n        or_replace: bool,\n        materialized: bool,\n        /// View name\n        name: ObjectName,\n        columns: Vec<Ident>,\n        query: Box<Query>,\n        with_options: Vec<SqlOption>,\n    },\n    /// CREATE TABLE\n    CreateTable {\n        or_replace: bool,\n        temporary: bool,\n        external: bool,\n        if_not_exists: bool,\n        /// Table name\n        name: ObjectName,\n        /// Optional schema\n        columns: Vec<ColumnDef>,\n        constraints: Vec<TableConstraint>,\n        hive_distribution: HiveDistributionStyle,\n        hive_formats: Option<HiveFormat>,\n        table_properties: Vec<SqlOption>,\n        with_options: Vec<SqlOption>,\n        file_format: Option<FileFormat>,\n        location: Option<String>,\n        query: Option<Box<Query>>,\n        without_rowid: bool,\n        like: Option<ObjectName>,\n    },\n    /// SQLite's `CREATE VIRTUAL TABLE .. USING <module_name> (<module_args>)`\n    CreateVirtualTable {\n        name: ObjectName,\n        if_not_exists: bool,\n        module_name: Ident,\n        module_args: Vec<Ident>,\n    },\n    /// CREATE INDEX\n    CreateIndex {\n        /// index name\n        name: ObjectName,\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        columns: Vec<OrderByExpr>,\n        unique: bool,\n        if_not_exists: bool,\n    },\n    /// ALTER TABLE\n    AlterTable {\n        /// Table name\n        name: ObjectName,\n        operation: AlterTableOperation,\n    },\n    /// DROP\n    Drop {\n        /// The type of the object to drop: TABLE, VIEW, etc.\n        object_type: ObjectType,\n        /// An optional `IF EXISTS` clause. (Non-standard.)\n        if_exists: bool,\n        /// One or more objects to drop. (ANSI SQL requires exactly one.)\n        names: Vec<ObjectName>,\n        /// Whether `CASCADE` was specified. This will be `false` when\n        /// `RESTRICT` or no drop behavior at all was specified.\n        cascade: bool,\n        /// Hive allows you specify whether the table's stored data will be\n        /// deleted along with the dropped table\n        purge: bool,\n    },\n    /// SET <variable>\n    ///\n    /// Note: this is not a standard SQL statement, but it is supported by at\n    /// least MySQL and PostgreSQL. Not all MySQL-specific syntatic forms are\n    /// supported yet.\n    SetVariable {\n        local: bool,\n        hivevar: bool,\n        variable: Ident,\n        value: Vec<SetVariableValue>,\n    },\n    /// SHOW <variable>\n    ///\n    /// Note: this is a PostgreSQL-specific statement.\n    ShowVariable { variable: Vec<Ident> },\n    /// SHOW CREATE TABLE\n    ///\n    /// Note: this is a MySQL-specific statement.\n    ShowCreate {\n        obj_type: ShowCreateObject,\n        obj_name: ObjectName,\n    },\n    /// SHOW COLUMNS\n    ///\n    /// Note: this is a MySQL-specific statement.\n    ShowColumns {\n        extended: bool,\n        full: bool,\n        table_name: ObjectName,\n        filter: Option<ShowStatementFilter>,\n    },\n    /// `{ BEGIN [ TRANSACTION | WORK ] | START TRANSACTION } ...`\n    StartTransaction { modes: Vec<TransactionMode> },\n    /// `SET TRANSACTION ...`\n    SetTransaction { modes: Vec<TransactionMode> },\n    /// `COMMIT [ TRANSACTION | WORK ] [ AND [ NO ] CHAIN ]`\n    Commit { chain: bool },\n    /// `ROLLBACK [ TRANSACTION | WORK ] [ AND [ NO ] CHAIN ]`\n    Rollback { chain: bool },\n    /// CREATE SCHEMA\n    CreateSchema {\n        schema_name: ObjectName,\n        if_not_exists: bool,\n    },\n    /// CREATE DATABASE\n    CreateDatabase {\n        db_name: ObjectName,\n        if_not_exists: bool,\n        location: Option<String>,\n        managed_location: Option<String>,\n    },\n    /// `ASSERT <condition> [AS <message>]`\n    Assert {\n        condition: Expr,\n        message: Option<Expr>,\n    },\n    /// `DEALLOCATE [ PREPARE ] { name | ALL }`\n    ///\n    /// Note: this is a PostgreSQL-specific statement.\n    Deallocate { name: Ident, prepare: bool },\n    /// `EXECUTE name [ ( parameter [, ...] ) ]`\n    ///\n    /// Note: this is a PostgreSQL-specific statement.\n    Execute { name: Ident, parameters: Vec<Expr> },\n    /// `PREPARE name [ ( data_type [, ...] ) ] AS statement`\n    ///\n    /// Note: this is a PostgreSQL-specific statement.\n    Prepare {\n        name: Ident,\n        data_types: Vec<DataType>,\n        statement: Box<Statement>,\n    },\n    /// EXPLAIN\n    Explain {\n        /// Carry out the command and show actual run times and other statistics.\n        analyze: bool,\n        // Display additional information regarding the plan.\n        verbose: bool,\n        /// A SQL query that specifies what to explain\n        statement: Box<Statement>,\n    },\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for Statement {\n    // Clippy thinks this function is too complicated, but it is painful to\n    // split up without extracting structs for each `Statement` variant.\n\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            Statement::Explain {\n                verbose,\n                analyze,\n                statement,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"EXPLAIN \")?;\n\n                if *analyze {\n                    write!(f, \"ANALYZE \")?;\n                }\n\n                if *verbose {\n                    write!(f, \"VERBOSE \")?;\n                }\n\n                write!(f, \"{}\", statement)\n            }\n            Statement::Query(s) => write!(f, \"{}\", s),\n            Statement::Directory {\n                overwrite,\n                local,\n                path,\n                file_format,\n                source,\n            } => {\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"INSERT{overwrite}{local} DIRECTORY '{path}'\",\n                    overwrite = if *overwrite { \" OVERWRITE\" } else { \"\" },\n                    local = if *local { \" LOCAL\" } else { \"\" },\n                    path = path\n                )?;\n                if let Some(ref ff) = file_format {\n                    write!(f, \" STORED AS {}\", ff)?\n                }\n                write!(f, \" {}\", source)\n            }\n            Statement::Msck {\n                table_name,\n                repair,\n                partition_action,\n            } => {\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"MSCK {repair}TABLE {table}\",\n                    repair = if *repair { \"REPAIR \" } else { \"\" },\n                    table = table_name\n                )?;\n                if let Some(pa) = partition_action {\n                    write!(f, \" {}\", pa)?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::Truncate {\n                table_name,\n                partitions,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"TRUNCATE TABLE {}\", table_name)?;\n                if let Some(ref parts) = partitions {\n                    if !parts.is_empty() {\n                        write!(f, \" PARTITION ({})\", display_comma_separated(parts))?;\n                    }\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::Analyze {\n                table_name,\n                partitions,\n                for_columns,\n                columns,\n                cache_metadata,\n                noscan,\n                compute_statistics,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"ANALYZE TABLE {}\", table_name)?;\n                if let Some(ref parts) = partitions {\n                    if !parts.is_empty() {\n                        write!(f, \" PARTITION ({})\", display_comma_separated(parts))?;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if *compute_statistics {\n                    write!(f, \" COMPUTE STATISTICS\")?;\n                }\n                if *noscan {\n                    write!(f, \" NOSCAN\")?;\n                }\n                if *cache_metadata {\n                    write!(f, \" CACHE METADATA\")?;\n                }\n                if *for_columns {\n                    write!(f, \" FOR COLUMNS\")?;\n                    if !columns.is_empty() {\n                        write!(f, \" {}\", display_comma_separated(columns))?;\n                    }\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::Insert {\n                or,\n                table_name,\n                overwrite,\n                partitioned,\n                columns,\n                after_columns,\n                source,\n                table,\n            } => {\n                if let Some(action) = or {\n                    write!(f, \"INSERT OR {} INTO {} \", action, table_name)?;\n                } else {\n                    write!(\n                        f,\n                        \"INSERT {act}{tbl} {table_name} \",\n                        table_name = table_name,\n                        act = if *overwrite { \"OVERWRITE\" } else { \"INTO\" },\n                        tbl = if *table { \" TABLE\" } else { \"\" }\n                    )?;\n                }\n                if !columns.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \"({}) \", display_comma_separated(columns))?;\n                }\n                if let Some(ref parts) = partitioned {\n                    if !parts.is_empty() {\n                        write!(f, \"PARTITION ({}) \", display_comma_separated(parts))?;\n                    }\n                }\n                if !after_columns.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \"({}) \", display_comma_separated(after_columns))?;\n                }\n                write!(f, \"{}\", source)\n            }\n\n            Statement::Copy {\n                table_name,\n                columns,\n                values,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"COPY {}\", table_name)?;\n                if !columns.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" ({})\", display_comma_separated(columns))?;\n                }\n                write!(f, \" FROM stdin; \")?;\n                if !values.is_empty() {\n                    writeln!(f)?;\n                    let mut delim = \"\";\n                    for v in values {\n                        write!(f, \"{}\", delim)?;\n                        delim = \"\\t\";\n                        if let Some(v) = v {\n                            write!(f, \"{}\", v)?;\n                        } else {\n                            write!(f, \"\\\\N\")?;\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                write!(f, \"\\n\\\\.\")\n            }\n            Statement::Update {\n                table_name,\n                assignments,\n                selection,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"UPDATE {}\", table_name)?;\n                if !assignments.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" SET {}\", display_comma_separated(assignments))?;\n                }\n                if let Some(selection) = selection {\n                    write!(f, \" WHERE {}\", selection)?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::Delete {\n                table_name,\n                selection,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"DELETE FROM {}\", table_name)?;\n                if let Some(selection) = selection {\n                    write!(f, \" WHERE {}\", selection)?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::CreateDatabase {\n                db_name,\n                if_not_exists,\n                location,\n                managed_location,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"CREATE\")?;\n                if *if_not_exists {\n                    write!(f, \" IF NOT EXISTS\")?;\n                }\n                write!(f, \" {}\", db_name)?;\n                if let Some(l) = location {\n                    write!(f, \" LOCATION '{}'\", l)?;\n                }\n                if let Some(ml) = managed_location {\n                    write!(f, \" MANAGEDLOCATION '{}'\", ml)?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::CreateView {\n                name,\n                or_replace,\n                columns,\n                query,\n                materialized,\n                with_options,\n            } => {\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"CREATE {or_replace}{materialized}VIEW {name}\",\n                    or_replace = if *or_replace { \"OR REPLACE \" } else { \"\" },\n                    materialized = if *materialized { \"MATERIALIZED \" } else { \"\" },\n                    name = name\n                )?;\n                if !with_options.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" WITH ({})\", display_comma_separated(with_options))?;\n                }\n                if !columns.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" ({})\", display_comma_separated(columns))?;\n                }\n                write!(f, \" AS {}\", query)\n            }\n            Statement::CreateTable {\n                name,\n                columns,\n                constraints,\n                table_properties,\n                with_options,\n                or_replace,\n                if_not_exists,\n                hive_distribution,\n                hive_formats,\n                external,\n                temporary,\n                file_format,\n                location,\n                query,\n                without_rowid,\n                like,\n            } => {\n                // We want to allow the following options\n                // Empty column list, allowed by PostgreSQL:\n                //   `CREATE TABLE t ()`\n                // No columns provided for CREATE TABLE AS:\n                //   `CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT a from t2`\n                // Columns provided for CREATE TABLE AS:\n                //   `CREATE TABLE t (a INT) AS SELECT a from t2`\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"CREATE {or_replace}{external}{temporary}TABLE {if_not_exists}{name}\",\n                    or_replace = if *or_replace { \"OR REPLACE \" } else { \"\" },\n                    external = if *external { \"EXTERNAL \" } else { \"\" },\n                    if_not_exists = if *if_not_exists { \"IF NOT EXISTS \" } else { \"\" },\n                    temporary = if *temporary { \"TEMPORARY \" } else { \"\" },\n                    name = name,\n                )?;\n                if !columns.is_empty() || !constraints.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" ({}\", display_comma_separated(columns))?;\n                    if !columns.is_empty() && !constraints.is_empty() {\n                        write!(f, \", \")?;\n                    }\n                    write!(f, \"{})\", display_comma_separated(constraints))?;\n                } else if query.is_none() && like.is_none() {\n                    // PostgreSQL allows `CREATE TABLE t ();`, but requires empty parens\n                    write!(f, \" ()\")?;\n                }\n                // Only for SQLite\n                if *without_rowid {\n                    write!(f, \" WITHOUT ROWID\")?;\n                }\n\n                // Only for Hive\n                if let Some(l) = like {\n                    write!(f, \" LIKE {}\", l)?;\n                }\n                match hive_distribution {\n                    HiveDistributionStyle::PARTITIONED { columns } => {\n                        write!(f, \" PARTITIONED BY ({})\", display_comma_separated(columns))?;\n                    }\n                    HiveDistributionStyle::CLUSTERED {\n                        columns,\n                        sorted_by,\n                        num_buckets,\n                    } => {\n                        write!(f, \" CLUSTERED BY ({})\", display_comma_separated(columns))?;\n                        if !sorted_by.is_empty() {\n                            write!(f, \" SORTED BY ({})\", display_comma_separated(sorted_by))?;\n                        }\n                        if *num_buckets > 0 {\n                            write!(f, \" INTO {} BUCKETS\", num_buckets)?;\n                        }\n                    }\n                    HiveDistributionStyle::SKEWED {\n                        columns,\n                        on,\n                        stored_as_directories,\n                    } => {\n                        write!(\n                            f,\n                            \" SKEWED BY ({})) ON ({})\",\n                            display_comma_separated(columns),\n                            display_comma_separated(on)\n                        )?;\n                        if *stored_as_directories {\n                            write!(f, \" STORED AS DIRECTORIES\")?;\n                        }\n                    }\n                    _ => (),\n                }\n\n                if let Some(HiveFormat {\n                    row_format,\n                    storage,\n                    location,\n                }) = hive_formats\n                {\n                    match row_format {\n                        Some(HiveRowFormat::SERDE { class }) => {\n                            write!(f, \" ROW FORMAT SERDE '{}'\", class)?\n                        }\n                        Some(HiveRowFormat::DELIMITED) => write!(f, \" ROW FORMAT DELIMITED\")?,\n                        None => (),\n                    }\n                    match storage {\n                        Some(HiveIOFormat::IOF {\n                            input_format,\n                            output_format,\n                        }) => write!(\n                            f,\n                            \" STORED AS INPUTFORMAT {} OUTPUTFORMAT {}\",\n                            input_format, output_format\n                        )?,\n                        Some(HiveIOFormat::FileFormat { format }) if !*external => {\n                            write!(f, \" STORED AS {}\", format)?\n                        }\n                        _ => (),\n                    }\n                    if !*external {\n                        if let Some(loc) = location {\n                            write!(f, \" LOCATION '{}'\", loc)?;\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n                if *external {\n                    write!(\n                        f,\n                        \" STORED AS {} LOCATION '{}'\",\n                        file_format.as_ref().unwrap(),\n                        location.as_ref().unwrap()\n                    )?;\n                }\n                if !table_properties.is_empty() {\n                    write!(\n                        f,\n                        \" TBLPROPERTIES ({})\",\n                        display_comma_separated(table_properties)\n                    )?;\n                }\n                if !with_options.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" WITH ({})\", display_comma_separated(with_options))?;\n                }\n                if let Some(query) = query {\n                    write!(f, \" AS {}\", query)?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::CreateVirtualTable {\n                name,\n                if_not_exists,\n                module_name,\n                module_args,\n            } => {\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"CREATE VIRTUAL TABLE {if_not_exists}{name} USING {module_name}\",\n                    if_not_exists = if *if_not_exists { \"IF NOT EXISTS \" } else { \"\" },\n                    name = name,\n                    module_name = module_name\n                )?;\n                if !module_args.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" ({})\", display_comma_separated(module_args))?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::CreateIndex {\n                name,\n                table_name,\n                columns,\n                unique,\n                if_not_exists,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"CREATE {unique}INDEX {if_not_exists}{name} ON {table_name}({columns})\",\n                unique = if *unique { \"UNIQUE \" } else { \"\" },\n                if_not_exists = if *if_not_exists { \"IF NOT EXISTS \" } else { \"\" },\n                name = name,\n                table_name = table_name,\n                columns = display_separated(columns, \",\")\n            ),\n            Statement::AlterTable { name, operation } => {\n                write!(f, \"ALTER TABLE {} {}\", name, operation)\n            }\n            Statement::Drop {\n                object_type,\n                if_exists,\n                names,\n                cascade,\n                purge,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"DROP {}{} {}{}{}\",\n                object_type,\n                if *if_exists { \" IF EXISTS\" } else { \"\" },\n                display_comma_separated(names),\n                if *cascade { \" CASCADE\" } else { \"\" },\n                if *purge { \" PURGE\" } else { \"\" }\n            ),\n            Statement::SetVariable {\n                local,\n                variable,\n                hivevar,\n                value,\n            } => {\n                f.write_str(\"SET \")?;\n                if *local {\n                    f.write_str(\"LOCAL \")?;\n                }\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"{hivevar}{name} = {value}\",\n                    hivevar = if *hivevar { \"HIVEVAR:\" } else { \"\" },\n                    name = variable,\n                    value = display_comma_separated(value)\n                )\n            }\n            Statement::ShowVariable { variable } => {\n                write!(f, \"SHOW\")?;\n                if !variable.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" {}\", display_separated(variable, \" \"))?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::ShowCreate { obj_type, obj_name } => {\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"SHOW CREATE {obj_type} {obj_name}\",\n                    obj_type = obj_type,\n                    obj_name = obj_name,\n                )?;\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::ShowColumns {\n                extended,\n                full,\n                table_name,\n                filter,\n            } => {\n                write!(\n                    f,\n                    \"SHOW {extended}{full}COLUMNS FROM {table_name}\",\n                    extended = if *extended { \"EXTENDED \" } else { \"\" },\n                    full = if *full { \"FULL \" } else { \"\" },\n                    table_name = table_name,\n                )?;\n                if let Some(filter) = filter {\n                    write!(f, \" {}\", filter)?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::StartTransaction { modes } => {\n                write!(f, \"START TRANSACTION\")?;\n                if !modes.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" {}\", display_comma_separated(modes))?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::SetTransaction { modes } => {\n                write!(f, \"SET TRANSACTION\")?;\n                if !modes.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \" {}\", display_comma_separated(modes))?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::Commit { chain } => {\n                write!(f, \"COMMIT{}\", if *chain { \" AND CHAIN\" } else { \"\" },)\n            }\n            Statement::Rollback { chain } => {\n                write!(f, \"ROLLBACK{}\", if *chain { \" AND CHAIN\" } else { \"\" },)\n            }\n            Statement::CreateSchema {\n                schema_name,\n                if_not_exists,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"CREATE SCHEMA {if_not_exists}{name}\",\n                if_not_exists = if *if_not_exists { \"IF NOT EXISTS \" } else { \"\" },\n                name = schema_name\n            ),\n            Statement::Assert { condition, message } => {\n                write!(f, \"ASSERT {}\", condition)?;\n                if let Some(m) = message {\n                    write!(f, \" AS {}\", m)?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::Deallocate { name, prepare } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"DEALLOCATE {prepare}{name}\",\n                prepare = if *prepare { \"PREPARE \" } else { \"\" },\n                name = name,\n            ),\n            Statement::Execute { name, parameters } => {\n                write!(f, \"EXECUTE {}\", name)?;\n                if !parameters.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \"({})\", display_comma_separated(parameters))?;\n                }\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Statement::Prepare {\n                name,\n                data_types,\n                statement,\n            } => {\n                write!(f, \"PREPARE {} \", name)?;\n                if !data_types.is_empty() {\n                    write!(f, \"({}) \", display_comma_separated(data_types))?;\n                }\n                write!(f, \"AS {}\", statement)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// SQL assignment `foo = expr` as used in SQLUpdate\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct Assignment {\n    pub id: Ident,\n    pub value: Expr,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for Assignment {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        write!(f, \"{} = {}\", self.id, self.value)\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum FunctionArg {\n    Named { name: Ident, arg: Expr },\n    Unnamed(Expr),\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for FunctionArg {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            FunctionArg::Named { name, arg } => write!(f, \"{} => {}\", name, arg),\n            FunctionArg::Unnamed(unnamed_arg) => write!(f, \"{}\", unnamed_arg),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// A function call\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct Function {\n    pub name: ObjectName,\n    pub args: Vec<FunctionArg>,\n    pub over: Option<WindowSpec>,\n    // aggregate functions may specify eg `COUNT(DISTINCT x)`\n    pub distinct: bool,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for Function {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        write!(\n            f,\n            \"{}({}{})\",\n            self.name,\n            if self.distinct { \"DISTINCT \" } else { \"\" },\n            display_comma_separated(&self.args),\n        )?;\n        if let Some(o) = &self.over {\n            write!(f, \" OVER ({})\", o)?;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// External table's available file format\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum FileFormat {\n    TEXTFILE,\n    SEQUENCEFILE,\n    ORC,\n    PARQUET,\n    AVRO,\n    RCFILE,\n    JSONFILE,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for FileFormat {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        use self::FileFormat::*;\n        f.write_str(match self {\n            TEXTFILE => \"TEXTFILE\",\n            SEQUENCEFILE => \"SEQUENCEFILE\",\n            ORC => \"ORC\",\n            PARQUET => \"PARQUET\",\n            AVRO => \"AVRO\",\n            RCFILE => \"RCFILE\",\n            JSONFILE => \"JSONFILE\",\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// A `LISTAGG` invocation `LISTAGG( [ DISTINCT ] <expr>[, <separator> ] [ON OVERFLOW <on_overflow>] ) )\n/// [ WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY <within_group1>[, ...] ) ]`\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct ListAgg {\n    pub distinct: bool,\n    pub expr: Box<Expr>,\n    pub separator: Option<Box<Expr>>,\n    pub on_overflow: Option<ListAggOnOverflow>,\n    pub within_group: Vec<OrderByExpr>,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for ListAgg {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        write!(\n            f,\n            \"LISTAGG({}{}\",\n            if self.distinct { \"DISTINCT \" } else { \"\" },\n            self.expr\n        )?;\n        if let Some(separator) = &self.separator {\n            write!(f, \", {}\", separator)?;\n        }\n        if let Some(on_overflow) = &self.on_overflow {\n            write!(f, \"{}\", on_overflow)?;\n        }\n        write!(f, \")\")?;\n        if !self.within_group.is_empty() {\n            write!(\n                f,\n                \" WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY {})\",\n                display_comma_separated(&self.within_group)\n            )?;\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n/// The `ON OVERFLOW` clause of a LISTAGG invocation\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum ListAggOnOverflow {\n    /// `ON OVERFLOW ERROR`\n    Error,\n\n    /// `ON OVERFLOW TRUNCATE [ <filler> ] WITH[OUT] COUNT`\n    Truncate {\n        filler: Option<Box<Expr>>,\n        with_count: bool,\n    },\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for ListAggOnOverflow {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        write!(f, \" ON OVERFLOW\")?;\n        match self {\n            ListAggOnOverflow::Error => write!(f, \" ERROR\"),\n            ListAggOnOverflow::Truncate { filler, with_count } => {\n                write!(f, \" TRUNCATE\")?;\n                if let Some(filler) = filler {\n                    write!(f, \" {}\", filler)?;\n                }\n                if *with_count {\n                    write!(f, \" WITH\")?;\n                } else {\n                    write!(f, \" WITHOUT\")?;\n                }\n                write!(f, \" COUNT\")\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum ObjectType {\n    Table,\n    View,\n    Index,\n    Schema,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for ObjectType {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        f.write_str(match self {\n            ObjectType::Table => \"TABLE\",\n            ObjectType::View => \"VIEW\",\n            ObjectType::Index => \"INDEX\",\n            ObjectType::Schema => \"SCHEMA\",\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum HiveDistributionStyle {\n    PARTITIONED {\n        columns: Vec<ColumnDef>,\n    },\n    CLUSTERED {\n        columns: Vec<Ident>,\n        sorted_by: Vec<ColumnDef>,\n        num_buckets: i32,\n    },\n    SKEWED {\n        columns: Vec<ColumnDef>,\n        on: Vec<ColumnDef>,\n        stored_as_directories: bool,\n    },\n    NONE,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum HiveRowFormat {\n    SERDE { class: String },\n    DELIMITED,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum HiveIOFormat {\n    IOF {\n        input_format: Expr,\n        output_format: Expr,\n    },\n    FileFormat {\n        format: FileFormat,\n    },\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct HiveFormat {\n    pub row_format: Option<HiveRowFormat>,\n    pub storage: Option<HiveIOFormat>,\n    pub location: Option<String>,\n}\n\nimpl Default for HiveFormat {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        HiveFormat {\n            row_format: None,\n            location: None,\n            storage: None,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub struct SqlOption {\n    pub name: Ident,\n    pub value: Value,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for SqlOption {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        write!(f, \"{} = {}\", self.name, self.value)\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum TransactionMode {\n    AccessMode(TransactionAccessMode),\n    IsolationLevel(TransactionIsolationLevel),\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for TransactionMode {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        use TransactionMode::*;\n        match self {\n            AccessMode(access_mode) => write!(f, \"{}\", access_mode),\n            IsolationLevel(iso_level) => write!(f, \"ISOLATION LEVEL {}\", iso_level),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum TransactionAccessMode {\n    ReadOnly,\n    ReadWrite,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for TransactionAccessMode {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        use TransactionAccessMode::*;\n        f.write_str(match self {\n            ReadOnly => \"READ ONLY\",\n            ReadWrite => \"READ WRITE\",\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum TransactionIsolationLevel {\n    ReadUncommitted,\n    ReadCommitted,\n    RepeatableRead,\n    Serializable,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for TransactionIsolationLevel {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        use TransactionIsolationLevel::*;\n        f.write_str(match self {\n            ReadUncommitted => \"READ UNCOMMITTED\",\n            ReadCommitted => \"READ COMMITTED\",\n            RepeatableRead => \"REPEATABLE READ\",\n            Serializable => \"SERIALIZABLE\",\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum ShowStatementFilter {\n    Like(String),\n    ILike(String),\n    Where(Expr),\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for ShowStatementFilter {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        use ShowStatementFilter::*;\n        match self {\n            Like(pattern) => write!(f, \"LIKE '{}'\", value::escape_single_quote_string(pattern)),\n            ILike(pattern) => write!(f, \"ILIKE {}\", value::escape_single_quote_string(pattern)),\n            Where(expr) => write!(f, \"WHERE {}\", expr),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum SetVariableValue {\n    Ident(Ident),\n    Literal(Value),\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for SetVariableValue {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        use SetVariableValue::*;\n        match self {\n            Ident(ident) => write!(f, \"{}\", ident),\n            Literal(literal) => write!(f, \"{}\", literal),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Sqlite specific syntax\n///\n/// https://sqlite.org/lang_conflict.html\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n#[cfg_attr(feature = \"serde\", derive(Serialize, Deserialize))]\npub enum SqliteOnConflict {\n    Rollback,\n    Abort,\n    Fail,\n    Ignore,\n    Replace,\n}\n\nimpl fmt::Display for SqliteOnConflict {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        use SqliteOnConflict::*;\n        match  Replace => write!(f, \"REPLACE\"),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n\n    #[test]\n    fn test_window_frame_default() {\n        let window_frame =
